Title: A Machine Learning Method to Infer Fundamental Stellar Parameters

Authors: Miller A.A., Bloom J.S., Richards J.W., Lee Y.S., Starr D.L.,

Table: SSPP Stellar Parameters for Hectospec Targets
================================================================================
Byte-by-byte Description of file: apj504861t3_mrt.txt
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
   Bytes Format Units    Label  Explanations
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
   1-  7 I7     ---      ID     Source identifier in the UWVSC 
   9- 12 F4.1   ---      P      Target priority for Hectospec observations
  14- 18 A5     ---      Flags  Analyis flags returned by the SSPP (1)
  20- 26 F7.1   K        Teff   Effective temperature (2)
  28- 34 F7.1   K       eTeff   Uncertainty in Teff  (2)
  36- 37 I2     ---    o_Teff   Number of methods used by SSPP to derive Teff
  39- 46 F8.2   [cm/s2]  log(g) Log surface gravity (2)
  48- 55 F8.2   [cm/s2] elog(g) Uncertainty in log(g) (2)
      57 I1     ---    o_log(g) Number of methods used by SSPP to derive log(g)
  59- 66 F8.2   [-]      [Fe/H] Metallicity (2)
  68- 75 F8.2   [-]     e[Fe/H] Uncertainty in [Fe/H] (2)
      77 I1     ---    o_[Fe/H] Number of methods used by SSPP to derive [Fe/H]
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Note (1): See Lee et al. 2008a.
Note (2): A -9999.00 indicates a NULL value.
